* <span data-ttu-id="a1472-109">R Server 8.0.5 - mainly a bug fix release.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-109">R Server 8.0.5 - mainly a bug fix release.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-110">See the [R Server Release Notes](https://msdn.microsoft.com/microsoft-r/notes/r-server-notes) for more info.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-110">See the [R Server Release Notes](https://msdn.microsoft.com/microsoft-r/notes/r-server-notes) for more info.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a1472-111">AzureML package on the edge node - [this R package](https://cran.r-project.org/web/packages/AzureML/vignettes/getting_started.html) enables R models to be published and consumed as an Azure ML web service.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-111">AzureML package on the edge node - [this R package](https://cran.r-project.org/web/packages/AzureML/vignettes/getting_started.html) enables R models to be published and consumed as an Azure ML web service.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="a1472-112">See the ["Operationalize a Model"](hdinsight-hadoop-r-server-overview.md#operationalize-a-model) section of our ["Overview of R Server on HDInsight"](hdinsight-hadoop-r-server-overview.md) article for more info.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-112">See the ["Operationalize a Model"](hdinsight-hadoop-r-server-overview.md#operationalize-a-model) section of our ["Overview of R Server on HDInsight"](hdinsight-hadoop-r-server-overview.md) article for more info.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a1472-113">Linux dependencies of the [top 100 most popular R packages](https://github.com/metacran/cranlogs) - these Linux package dependencies are now pre-installed.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-113">Linux dependencies of the [top 100 most popular R packages](https://github.com/metacran/cranlogs) - these Linux package dependencies are now pre-installed.</span></span>

### <a name="dos--donts-between-cluster-versions"></a><span data-ttu-id="a1472-1465">Do's & Dont's between cluster versions</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1465">Do's & Dont's between cluster versions</span></span>

### <a name="breaking-changes"></a><span data-ttu-id="a1472-1473">Breaking changes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1473">Breaking changes</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="a1472-1474">**Prefix syntax**: Only the "wasbs://" syntax is supported in HDInsight 3.1 and 3.0 clusters.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1474">**Prefix syntax**: Only the "wasbs://" syntax is supported in HDInsight 3.1 and 3.0 clusters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1475">The older "asv://" syntax is supported in HDInsight 2.1 and 1.6 clusters, but it is not supported in HDInsight 3.1 or 3.0 clusters.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1475">The older "asv://" syntax is supported in HDInsight 2.1 and 1.6 clusters, but it is not supported in HDInsight 3.1 or 3.0 clusters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1476">This means that any jobs submitted to an HDInsight 3.1  or 3.0 cluster that explicitly use the "asv://" syntax will fail.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1476">This means that any jobs submitted to an HDInsight 3.1  or 3.0 cluster that explicitly use the "asv://" syntax will fail.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1477">The "wasbs://" syntax should be used instead.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1477">The "wasbs://" syntax should be used instead.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1478">Also, jobs submitted to any HDInsight 3.1 or 3.0 clusters that are created with an existing metastore that contains explicit references to resources using the "asv://" syntax will fail.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1478">Also, jobs submitted to any HDInsight 3.1 or 3.0 clusters that are created with an existing metastore that contains explicit references to resources using the "asv://" syntax will fail.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1479">These metastores need to be re-created using the "wasbs://" syntax to address resources.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1479">These metastores need to be re-created using the "wasbs://" syntax to address resources.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a1472-1480">**Ports**: The ports used by the HDInsight service have changed.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1480">**Ports**: The ports used by the HDInsight service have changed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1481">The port numbers that were being used were within the ephemeral port range of the Windows operating system.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1481">The port numbers that were being used were within the ephemeral port range of the Windows operating system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1482">Ports are allocated automatically from a predefined ephemeral range for short-lived Internet protocol-based communications.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1482">Ports are allocated automatically from a predefined ephemeral range for short-lived Internet protocol-based communications.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1483">The new set of allowed Hortonworks Data Platform (HDP) service port numbers are outside this range to avoid encountering conflicts that could arise with the ports used by services running on the head node.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1483">The new set of allowed Hortonworks Data Platform (HDP) service port numbers are outside this range to avoid encountering conflicts that could arise with the ports used by services running on the head node.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1484">The new port numbers should not cause any breaking changes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1484">The new port numbers should not cause any breaking changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1485">The numbers used are as follows:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1485">The numbers used are as follows:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="a1472-1626">Release notes for the Hortonworks Data Platforms (HDPs) that are used by HDInsight version clusters are available at the following locations:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1626">Release notes for the Hortonworks Data Platforms (HDPs) that are used by HDInsight version clusters are available at the following locations:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1627">HDInsight version 3.1 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.7][hdp-2-1-7].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1627">HDInsight version 3.1 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.7][hdp-2-1-7].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1628">This is the default Hadoop cluster created when using the Azure portal after 11/7/2014.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1628">This is the default Hadoop cluster created when using the Azure portal after 11/7/2014.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1629">HDInsight 3.1 clusters created before 11/7/2014 were based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.1][hdp-2-1-1]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1629">HDInsight 3.1 clusters created before 11/7/2014 were based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.1][hdp-2-1-1]</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1630">HDInsight version 3.0 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.0][hdp-2-0-8].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1630">HDInsight version 3.0 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.0][hdp-2-0-8].</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1631">HDInsight version 2.1 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 1.3][hdp-1-3-0].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1631">HDInsight version 2.1 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 1.3][hdp-1-3-0].</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="a1472-1632">HDInsight version 1.6 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 1.1][hdp-1-1-0].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="a1472-1632">HDInsight version 1.6 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on the [Hortonworks Data Platform 1.1][hdp-1-1-0].</span></span>
